NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

Notice
NOTICE UNDER SECTION 485 OF THE COMPANIES ACT, 1956
In the matter of Section 484(1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956
&
In the matter of Textile Eco Solutions Tamilnadu Limited having Registered Office at 62,
Appachi Nagar Main Road, Kongu Nagar, Tiruppur-641 607
Notice is hereby of given that a Special Resolution was passed at the Extraordinary General Meeting held on
7-1-2013 at the Registered Office of the Company to Wind-up Voluntarily the above named Company under Section
484(1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956 and Shri P. Vidhyaprakash has been appointed as Liquidator under Section 490 of
the said Act.
Dated 7th day January 2013 at Tiruppur.
Chennai,

P. VIDHYAPRAKASH

14th February 2013.

Liquidator.
